        (1): BatchNorm2d(96, eps=0.001, momentum=0.03, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
      )
      (rbr_1x1): Sequential(
        (0): Conv2d(96, 96, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1), bias=False)
        (1): BatchNorm2d(96, eps=0.001, momentum=0.03, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
      )
    )
    (108): Concat()
    (109): Conv(
      (conv): Conv2d(752, 184, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1), bias=False)
      (bn): BatchNorm2d(184, eps=0.001, momentum=0.03, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
      (act): SiLU()
    )
    (110): RepConv(
      (act): SiLU()
      (rbr_dense): Sequential(
        (0): Conv2d(48, 96, kernel_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1, 1), bias=False)
        (1): BatchNorm2d(96, eps=0.001, momentum=0.03, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
      )
      (rbr_1x1): Sequential(
        (0): Conv2d(48, 96, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1), bias=False)
        (1): BatchNorm2d(96, eps=0.001, momentum=0.03, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
      )
    )
    (111): RepConv(
      (act): SiLU()
      (rbr_dense): Sequential(
        (0): Conv2d(96, 184, kernel_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1, 1), bias=False)
        (1): BatchNorm2d(184, eps=0.001, momentum=0.03, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
      )
      (rbr_1x1): Sequential(

        (1): BatchNorm2d(184, eps=0.001, momentum=0.03, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
      )
    )
    (112): RepConv(
      (act): SiLU()
      (rbr_dense): Sequential(
        (0): Conv2d(184, 360, kernel_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1, 1), bias=False)
        (1): BatchNorm2d(360, eps=0.001, momentum=0.03, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
      )
      (rbr_1x1): Sequential(

        (1): BatchNorm2d(360, eps=0.001, momentum=0.03, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
      )
    )
    (113): YOLOXDetect(
      (stems): ModuleList(
        (0): Conv(
          (conv): Conv2d(96, 96, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1), bias=False)
          (bn): BatchNorm2d(96, eps=0.001, momentum=0.03, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)

        )

          (bn): BatchNorm2d(96, eps=0.001, momentum=0.03, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)

        )

          (bn): BatchNorm2d(96, eps=0.001, momentum=0.03, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
          (act): SiLU()
        )
      )
      (cls_convs): ModuleList(
        (0-2): 3 x RepConv(
          (act): SiLU()
          (rbr_identity): BatchNorm2d(96, eps=0.001, momentum=0.03, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)

            (1): BatchNorm2d(96, eps=0.001, momentum=0.03, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
          )
          (rbr_1x1): Sequential(

            (1): BatchNorm2d(96, eps=0.001, momentum=0.03, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
          )
        )
      )
      (reg_convs): ModuleList(
        (0-2): 3 x RepConv(
          (act): SiLU()
          (rbr_identity): BatchNorm2d(96, eps=0.001, momentum=0.03, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
          (rbr_dense): Sequential(

            (1): BatchNorm2d(96, eps=0.001, momentum=0.03, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)

            (1): BatchNorm2d(96, eps=0.001, momentum=0.03, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
          )
        )
      )
      (cls_preds): ModuleList(
        (0-2): 3 x Conv2d(96, 2, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1))
      )
      (reg_preds): ModuleList(
        (0-2): 3 x Conv2d(96, 4, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1))
      )
      (obj_preds): ModuleList(

      )
      (ia): ModuleList(
        (0-2): 3 x ImplicitA()
      )
      (im): ModuleList(
        (0-2): 3 x ImplicitM()
      )
    )
  )
